MyLowes
Rewards Program 





</u></span><br></p><p>The MyLowes Rewards Program provides MLR Members with certain benefits and offers (as described further herein) (collectively <b>MyLowes Rewards</b>), unless prohibited by applicable law, based on Personal Account Holders accrued spend on Eligible Purchases (as defined below) or other actions or opportunities as may be presented by Lowes from time to time in Lowes sole discretion. MLR Members are placed in MyLowes Rewards Statuses (as defined below) based on the MLR Members accrued spend. The MyLowes Rewards Statuses determine the rate a MLR Member earns points on Eligible Purchases towards MyLowes Money rewards (<b>MyLowes Money</b>) that can be applied towards future Lowes purchases and may determine other benefits.&nbsp;</p><p>There is no fee associated with the MyLowes Rewards Program. Your participation in the MyLowes Rewards Program is unique to the MLR Members Personal Account. MyLowes Rewards Program. MyLowes Rewards, MyLowes Rewards Statuses, and My Points, and MyLowes Money may not be gifted, purchased, sold, bartered, brokered or otherwise transferred.&nbsp;</p><p></p><p>MyLowes Rewards, including My Points and MyLowes Money available via the MyLowes Rewards Program, have no cash value, are purely promotional and do not constitute property of any MLR Member. No portion of any payment for Eligible Purchases under the MyLowes Rewards Program or any MyLowes Rewards Status, member benefits, or any other MyLowes Rewards constitutes consideration paid for the MyLowes Rewards Program or any MyLowes Rewards benefit. Lowes reserves the right in its sole discretion to limit the claiming or redemption of specific MyLowes Rewards and to limit the number of MyLowes Reward Statuses and MyLowes Rewards available.</p><p></p><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Rewards Program Period.</span> MyLowes Rewards Program is voluntary and based on consecutive MyLowes Rewards Program Periods (as defined herein), starting in the year in which a MLR Member joins MyLowes Rewards. The initial MyLowes Rewards Program Period is effective on the date the MyLowes Rewards Program becomes available in your area (see Program Rollout and Location Launch Calendar below) to December 31, 2024. Each subsequent MyLowes Rewards Program Period will be effective January 1 to December 31 of each calendar year, unless otherwise stated herein (each separate calendar year is a <span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Rewards Program Period</span>). Lowes may, in its sole and exclusive discretion, designate different MyLowes Rewards Program Periods or modify, shorten or extend any MyLowes Rewards Program Period. Eligible Purchases accrued spend expires at 12:01 a.m. ET on January 1 each Program Period.</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Distribution of Benefits.</span> All benefits and/or MyLowes Rewards, including MyLowes Money, generated will accrue during a MyLowes Rewards Program Period and will be auto-issued only to the Registered User of the Personal Account. For avoidance of doubt, MyLowes Rewards, including any My Points and MyLowes Money (as defined herein), shall only accrue and be distributed to the Personal Account identified at the time of purchase.<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Program Launch. </span>Registered Users will be notified via email as to the start of the MyLowes Rewards Program in their respective area.<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Withdrawing From MyLowes Rewards Program.</span> If you are enrolled in the MyLowes Rewards Program and decide to deactivate or cancel your Personal Account, you will lose access to any stored information in your Personal Account, accrued and unused benefits, including any unused MyLowes Money saved in your Wallet. If you wish to deactivate your Account or delete your information, please contact us at 1-800-445-6937.<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Eligible Purchases: </span><span style="font-weight: bold;">Eligible Purchases</span> are MyLowes Tracked Purchases that have been settled and fulfilled and appear on the Personal Account purchase history excluding: rental fees; labor services and special fees; warranties; Lowes Protection Plans; shipping and handling; delivery; surcharges; service fees; sales and use taxes; product fees, purchases of Lowes Gift Cards or other third-party Gift Cards,&nbsp; or purchases or transactions made with MyLowes Rewards, including MyLowes Money, or other promotional items (such as free items), or purchases made using payment tender currently saved to an existing PRO Account.<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Rewards Program Status.</span> The MyLowes Rewards Program has different membership levels (each a <span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Rewards Status</span>), which is based on the MLR Members cumulative, accrued spend on Eligible Purchases in the applicable MyLowes Rewards Program Period. See <span style="font-weight: bold;">Table 2.2</span> below for the spend thresholds for each Status. MLR Members can reach one or more of the following MyLowes Rewards Program Statuses within a given MyLowes Rewards Program Period: Bronze Key, Silver Key, Gold Key. Each Status provides MLR Members with access to unique MyLowes Rewards Program benefits and offers, including lower spend threshold to receive free shipping, as discussed in detail below. Lowes in its sole discretion, may provide certain MLR Members with Silver Key Status based on criteria other than cumulative, accrued spend on Eligible Purchases. In such instances, these customers must still meet the accrued spend threshold in <span style="font-weight: bold;">Table 2.2</span> to achieve the next Status. For example, a MLR Member receives Silver Key Status at a time MLR Member has $0 in accrued Eligible Purchase spend; such MLR Member must reach $2,000 of Eligible Purchase spend to achieve Gold Key Status.<br><br>During a MyLowes Rewards Program Period, MLR Member may move up into one or more MyLowes Rewards Statuses based on the MLR Members accrued Eligible Purchases. Once a MLR Member reaches a certain MyLowes Rewards Status, the MLR Member will maintain that MyLowes Status for the remainder of the MyLowes Rewards Program Period and the subsequent MyLowes Rewards Program Period provided Eligible Purchases are not returned. If a MLR Member does not make enough Eligible Purchases by the end of a given MyLowes Rewards Program Period to maintain the MyLowes Rewards Status reached the previous MyLowes Reward Program Period, then the MLR Member will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower MyLowes Rewards Status that corresponds to the MLR Members actual accrued spend from Eligible Purchases made in the preceding MyLowes Rewards Program Period. A MLR Members Eligible Purchase accrued spend will reset to zero at the beginning of each new MyLowes Rewards Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each MyLowes Rewards Status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required) and determine a MLR Members starting MyLowes Rewards Status for any MyLowes Rewards Program Period in its sole discretion.<br><br></li><li><b>Lower Threshold for Free Standard Shipping Benefit (Not Available in AK &amp; HI).</b> MLR Members may receive free standard shipping on eligible purchases if they meet a minimum purchase threshold. For example, MLR Members in the Bronze Key Status will receive free standard shipping on eligible purchases of $35 or more, subject to certain exclusions. MLR Members in the Silver and Gold Key Statuses will receive free standard shipping on eligible purchases without any minimum spend required. The lower free standard shipping threshold is only applicable to eligible purchases made through Lowes.com while a MLR Member is logged into their MyLowes Rewards Account. See <b>Table 2.2</b> below for the minimum purchase thresholds a MLR Member must meet for each Status to receive free standard shipping on purchase orders. Standard shipping and Free Standard Shipping are not available in Alaska and Hawaii.</li></ul><p></p><p></p><ul class="list-disc"></ul><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="GridStyles__GridColumn-sc-1ejksnu-2 jVtdnu col sc-1t79ojw_engage-common-1 exSWev sm-12 md-12 lg-12 xl-12"><div class="nvl2lw_engage-common-0 fmiIDq" data-techname="TextBlock" style=&quot;font-weight"><h2 class="styles__H2-sc-11vpuyu-1 irzRON typography variant--h2 align--left section-header" color="text_primary" id=""></h2><div data-linkid="&lt;ul class=&quot;list-disc&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-weight" class="ifxsfn_engage-common-0 eWBThw"><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">My Points.</span> MLR Members will earn points on Eligible Purchases in accordance with their MyLowes Status (<b>My Points</b>).&nbsp; My Points expire if no Eligible Purchases are made, and no My Points are otherwise earned or awarded to the Account, for 365 days.</li><ul class="list-circle"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">My Points Calculation.</span>&nbsp;<br>My Points will be awarded on Eligible Purchases in accordance with a MLR Members corresponding MyLowes Status. MLR Members in the Bronze Key Status will earn 1 My Point per dollar spent on an Eligible Purchases; MLR Members in the Silver Key Status will earn 1.25 My Points per dollar spent on Eligible Purchases; and MLR Members in the Gold Key Status will earn 1.5 My Points per dollar spent on an Eligible Purchases. For illustrative purposes only, if a MLR Member in Silver Status made a $95 Eligible Purchase, the approximate number of My Points awarded would be 118.75 My Points.<br><br>Each MyLowes Rewards Status and the My Points accrual rate is progressive, meaning the applicable percentage will only apply to the Eligible Purchase amount MLR Member spent within the applicable Status. Lowes will round partial cents to the nearest cent. Two different My Points accrual percentages may apply to one Eligible Purchase. By way of example only, if a MLR Member needed $50 in in Eligible Purchases to move up to a higher MyLowes Status and spent $100 on a Eligible Purchase, $50 of such Eligible Purchase will earn My Points at the lower MyLowes Rewards Status and the remaining $50 will earn My Points at the higher MyLowes Rewards Status.<br><br>Lowes in its sole
discretion may offer additional points or a higher rate of points per dollar
spent for certain or select Eligible Purchases. When expressed as a multiplier
of My Points, the My Points awarded will be calculated by multiplying the
Eligible Purchase amount (accounting for MLR Members Status) by the stated
multiplier. For example, A Silver Key Status MLR Member makes a $100 Eligible
Purchase with a 2X My Points offer; this MLR Member would earn 250 My Points
($100 x 1.25 x 2 = 250).<br></li><li>&nbsp;<b>Returns of Eligible Purchases.</b>
If an item(s) from an Eligible Purchase is returned, the returned amount will
be deducted from Eligible Purchase accrued spend and My Points. If a return is
made after MyLowes Money has been issued, a MLR Members Account may reflect a
negative My Points balance.



<br></li></ul></ul><p></p><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Additional My Points Offerings.</span> From time to time, Lowes, or others acting with our permission, may offer MLR Members opportunities to earn My Points for engaging in certain promotional activities; upon achieving certain MyLowes Rewards Program milestones; or completing other actions or opportunities as may be presented. My Points for such offerings will be awarded as described in the applicable offer and will be subject to any additional terms set forth within that offer.</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Rewards Credit Card Holder Benefit.</span> MyLowes Rewards Credit Card (MLRCC) holders will be upgraded to Silver Key Status, and have access to Silver Key benefits, when their LAC is saved to their MyLowes Rewards Wallet. Certain LAC holders may need to save their LAC card to their MyLowes Reward Wallet themselves by following the instructions on the Site. If&nbsp; MLR Member terminates their LAC credit line, the MLR Members MyLowes Status will be placed in the MyLowes Rewards Status that matches their current Eligible Purchases spend accrual. For example, if MLR Member terminates their LAC credit line, and MLR Members spend threshold matches Bronze Key, then, the MLR Member will be moved from the Silver Key Status to the Bronze Key Status.<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MyLowes Money.&nbsp;</span> MLR Members will be automatically issued MyLowes Money to their Wallet in $5 increments when a MLR Member accrues 1,000 My Points and those My Points will be deducted from the MLR Members My Points balance. MyLowes Money can be applied towards future purchases that are made on or&nbsp; before the expiration date set forth on each MyLowes Money certificate. If not used within the redemption period, then the MyLowes Money expires. If no redemption period or expiration date is stated, then the expiration date will be thirty (30) days from date of its issuance.<br></li><ul class="list-circle"><li>MyLowes Money is non-transferrable and is not a credit, debit or gift card; it has no implied warranties. <span style="font-weight: bold;">There is a limit of 5 MyLowes Money per transaction.</span> MyLowes Money will be applied to a MLR Members purchase after all applicable discounts, coupons, taxes and fees have been applied. MyLowes Money cannot be exchanged for cash, is void if altered, defaced, copied, transferred, or sold (thru any on-line auction or otherwise). MyLowes Money may not be redeemed or used on (1) gift cards, including Lowes-branded gift cards; (2) payments to a Lowes credit card or any third-party charge account; (3) on any Lowes branded website operated by a 3rd party; or (4) Weber, Kichler or Miele products. <span style="font-weight: bold;">Returns: for merchandise purchased with MyLowes Money return value will be applied first to payment method and any remaining value will be returned as MyLowes Money to customers Wallet.</span></li><li>A MLR Member may use a partial amount of their MyLowes Money, but the MLR Member cannot dictate the amount of MyLowes Money that will be applied towards a purchase (i.e., a MLR Member cannot decide to use a pre-determined amount of MyLowes Money on a purchase). If a MLR Member purchases a $3.00 product and uses $3.00 out of the $5.00 available on the MyLowes Money certificate, the MLR Member can later apply the remaining $2.00 towards a future purchase that is made within the applicable redemption period.</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Returns with MyLowes Money.</span> MLR Members who return an item that was purchased with MyLowes Money will receive the MyLowes Money back to their Account&nbsp; or in the form of one or more In-store Credit (Merchandise Credit) cards in Lowes discretion. If the MyLowes Money that was used to make the purchase has expired and Lowes issues replacement MyLowes Money, your MyLowes Money will be returned to the Wallet with an updated expiration date. For returns of orders partially paid with MyLowes Money, MLR Members will first receive the returned payment to their payment method (cash, credit or debit card) and then any remaining amount will be returned to the MLR Members Wallet as MyLowes Money or in the form of one or more In-store Credit (Merchandise Credit) cards in Lowes discretion.</li></ul><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expiration of Benefits; Inactive Accounts.</span> At the end of each MyLowes Rewards Program Period, a MLR Members accrued Eligible Purchases balance will reset to $0.00. Unclaimed or unused MyLowes Rewards, including MyLowes Money, expire upon the exit, cancellation or termination of your MyLowes Rewards Account as described below. If you have any questions regarding your MyLowes Rewards Account status, please contact Lowes by calling 1-800-445-6937.&nbsp;<br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Suspension or Termination.</span> Lowes reserves the right to terminate or suspend a Registered Users Personal Account if the Personal Account remains inactive for a period of two (2) years or more. Accordingly, if a MLR Member does not make an Eligible Purchase within a two (2) year time period after the MLR Members initial Account creation or a MLR Members last recorded Eligible Purchase, whichever occurs later, Lowes reserves the right to terminate or suspend the Registered Users Personal Account. You understand and agree that the termination or suspension by Lowes of a Personal Account will result in the cancellation of all MyLowes Rewards Benefits.<br></li><li>Lowes reserves the right in its sole discretion to update, change, modify, add, end, delete, suspend or terminate the MyLowes Rewards Program or any or all benefits under the MyLowes Rewards Program or any policy pertaining to the MyLowes Rewards Program, at any time, for any reason, including our right to discontinue or change the MyLowes Statuses or change the expiration date or claiming or redemption value of My Points or MyLowes Money, merge the MyLowes Rewards Program with another program, or adjust how My Points or MyLowes Money are received, calculated or claimed.<br></li><li>If Lowes elects to terminate or modify in a material way the MyLowes Rewards Program or any benefits or policies of the MyLowes Rewards Program, Lowes will provide a notice of the material modification or termination by posting the modifications or notice of termination to Lowes.com. We encourage you to review these Terms regularly for modifications. Please consult your tax adviser concerning any tax consequences that may arise from your participation.<br></li><li><b>Customer Service.</b>&nbsp;For MyLowes Rewards Program assistance, please contact <a href="tel:18004456937" title="tel:18004456937">1-800-445-6937</a> for MyLowes Rewards.<br></li></ul><p></p><p></p><ul class="list-disc"></ul><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-1f1s622_engage-common-2 kNOjmZ"><div style="display:contents"><div class="GridStyles__GridRow-sc-1ejksnu-1 qwBjG row sc-1t79ojw_engage-common-0 dJXoLs justify-center"><div class="GridStyles__GridColumn-sc-1ejksnu-2 jVtdnu col sc-1t79ojw_engage-common-1 exSWev sm-12 md-12 lg-12 xl-12"><div class="nvl2lw_engage-common-0 fmiIDq" data-techname="TextBlock" data-businessname="na" data-componenttitle="Additional PRO Account and MVPs Terms" data-triggerimpression="false" data-trigger="false" data-gaugelinkid="&lt;h2&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: unset; background-colo"><h2 class="styles__H2-sc-11vpuyu-1 irzRON typography variant--h2 align--left section-header" color="text_primary" id="AdditionalPROAccountandMVPsTerms">Additional PRO Account and MVPs Terms</h2><div data-linkid="&lt;h2&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: unset; background-colo" class="ifxsfn_engage-common-0 eWBThw"><h2><span style="font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;"></span></h2><h2></h2><h2></h2><p><b style="font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;">PRO Account Specific Benefits.&nbsp;</b><span style="font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;">A PRO Account may be required to obtain and use certain site features, programs and benefits, including but not limited to the MVPs Pro Rewards &amp; Partnership Program, Bulk Purchasing, and Pro Exclusive Pricing. Converting a Personal Account into a PRO Account will result in the loss of certain benefits exclusive to Personal Accounts, including Military Discount, Subscriptions and MyLowes features, and any other benefits unique to Personal Accounts.</p><p>These PRO Terms do not alter the terms and conditions of any other written agreement you may have with Lowes for other products and services.</p><p><b>PRO Accounts.</b> PRO Accounts must be registered under a business name (the <b>Organization</b>). An individual User with authority to bind the Organization may create a single Account for an Organization (<b>Primary Admin</b>), and any other admin may invite others to create additional user Accounts as part of the Organization. To have multiple Users under a single Organization Account, the Primary Admin&nbsp;must invite those users to register using the email link, code provided through your PRO Account or other methods as determined by Lowes. A credit or debit card can only be registered to the MVPs Pro Rewards Program for one Organization. Attempts to register the same tender to multiple Organizations may result in limited benefits or functionality. All&nbsp;<span style="background-color: transparent; font-size: unset;">Rewards associated with a Registered Tender belong to the Organization and not the User registering the card.</span></p><p>By creating a PRO Account, you represent and warrant to Lowes that you are fully authorized to create and manage that Account on behalf of the company associated with that Account.</p><p><b>PRO Account Eligibility and Restrictions. </b>PRO Accounts are available only to business customers in the 50 United States (and DC). Personal use is prohibited. The terms of any written contract or agreement with any Government, GPO Parent Organization, National Account or Managed Account customer shall supersede any conflicting terms herein. Customers who self-identify as government organizations will be opted out of Program by default and must opt-in eligible to receive Rewards.</p><p>PRO Accounts and the MVPs Pro Rewards Program are not available and each is void where prohibited by federal, state or local law.</p><p>Unless expressly provided therein and except for Lowes Every Day 5% Credit discount offer, the PRO Account, the MVPs Pro Rewards Program, or any subprogram offers and benefits cannot be combined with any (i) other promotion, discount, markdown, coupon, rebate or offer, including any Lowes volume or special discount programs (such as but not limited to Contractor Packs, Buy in Bulk, Volume Savings Program (<b>VSP</b>), Military Discount, Employee Discount,&nbsp;<a href="/l/about/lowest-price-guarantee" title="/l/about/lowest-price-guarantee">Lowest Price Guarantee</a>, Special Value, New Lower Price, Was:Now and credit discount offers); or (ii) associate-discretion price adjustments.</p><p><b>Notice of Benefits/Incentives for Account Maintenance.&nbsp;</b>To receive MVPs Pro Rewards Program membership benefits, including but not limited to PRO Tracked Purchases (as defined below), you must maintain a PRO Account. Some Program membership benefits are earned via qualifying purchases. Organizations are placed in MVPs Levels (as defined below) based on their Users accrued spend, and the MVPs Levels determine the level of Rewards an Organization earns, as more fully described below. For more information on MVPs Levels, Rewards and Program features and experiences, please visit the <a href="https://www.lowes.com/Pro">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page.</a></li></ul><ul><ul class="list-circle"><li>There is no fee associated with the Program. Your participation in the Program is unique to the Organization under which you are registered for the Program. MVPs Levels and Rewards may not be gifted, purchased, sold, bartered, brokered or otherwise transferred, except that the Program may allow a Primary Admin on behalf of the Organization to allocate certain Rewards in certain limited instances as described below. Rewards available via the MVPs Program have no cash value, are purely promotional and do not constitute property of any User or Organization (as applicable). No portion of any payment for purchases qualifying for the Program or any MVPs Level, Member Benefits or Rewards constitutes consideration paid for the Program or any MVPs Level or Rewards. Lowes reserves the right in its sole discretion to limit the claiming or redemption of specific Rewards and to limit the number of MVPs Levels and Rewards available.</li></ul></ul><ul class="list-disc"><li><b style="background-color: transparent;">MVPs Pro Rewards Program Periods.</b><span style="background-color: transparent;"> Participation in the Program is based on consecutive Program Periods, starting in the year in which an Organization joins the MVPs Pro Rewards Program. The initial Program Period is effective from Jan. 7, 2022 to Dec. 31, 2022. Each subsequent Program Period will begin on January 1 of the applicable calendar year.</span></li><li>At the end of each Program Period, all unclaimed Rewards and Member Benefits will be forfeited, subject to the exclusions set forth below. Lowes may, in its sole and exclusive discretion, designate a different Program Period or modify, suspend, shorten or extend a Program Period with respect to the Program.</li><li><b style="background-color: transparent;">MVPs Pro Rewards Program Eligibility.</b><span style="background-color: transparent;"> In order to be eligible for the Program, you must have a PRO Account. Government customers and cooperative purchasing programs, including GPOs Parent Organizations, are not eligible for the Program. Resellers are expressly excluded from the MVPs Pro Rewards Program. Commercial customers with a National Account contract are not eligible for MVPs Earn Back Rewards.</span></li><li><b>MVPs Pro Rewards Program Qualifying Purchases.</b>&nbsp;Qualifying purchases include net completed purchases of qualifying products as further detailed below and subject to the exclusions below (Qualifying&nbsp;Purchases). Completed purchases means the transaction has been settled and fulfilled and the transaction appears on the Organizations Account purchase history. Qualifying Purchases are PRO Tracked Purchases calculated based on the actual amount paid on any completed purchases of products made by the Organization during the Program Period after any allowable discounts are applied, if any, and excluding: labor services and special fees; warranty; Lowes Protection Plans; shipping and handling; delivery; surcharges; service fees; sales and use taxes; and product fees. Qualifying Purchases do not include: (i) purchases of electrical cable and electrical wires; (ii) purchases of Lowes Gift Cards or Gift Certificates or other third-party Gift Cards or Gift Certificates; (iii) purchases made using an employee discount (iv) purchases or transactions made with Rewards or other promotional items (such as free items), whether made in store, online or through the Lowes app; (v) government purchases; (vi) purchases made for personal use, including any purchase using a Personal Account or Military Discount; or (vii) purchases made on tender previously registered by another Organization. In addition, any purchase of Paint (as defined below) will be a Qualifying Purchase only for the purposes of determining MVPs Level but will not be a Qualifying Purchase for purposes of calculating MVPs Earn Back Rewards.</li></ul><ul><ul class="list-disc"><li>If an item from a Qualifying Purchase is returned, the return amount will be deducted from Qualifying Purchase spend toward earning Rewards. If the item is returned after a Reward has been issued, your Account may reflect a negative balance.</li><li>For a new PRO Account, once your Account is created, Lowes will recognize any Qualifying Purchase made online while logged into your Account and any Qualifying Purchase made in store while using Registered Tender or Member ID.</li><li>Qualifying Purchases made between the date of confirmed MVPs Earn Back Rewards eligibility and 12/31/22 will count toward the MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation as defined below.</li></ul></ul><ul class="list-disc"><li><b>MVPs Levels. </b>Each Organization can reach one or more MVPs Levels: MVPs, Silver MVPs, Gold MVPs, Platinum MVPs (each, an <b>MVPs Level</b>) based on the accrued spend within a given Program Period from that Organizations Users Qualifying Purchases. Details regarding the MVPs Levels are available through the <a href="/l/Pro/pro-benefits" title="/l/Pro/pro-benefits">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page</a>. Upon joining the Program, an Organization will be placed in the lowest MVPs Level. As an Organizations Users make Qualifying Purchases during the applicable Program Period, the Organization may move up into one or more MVPs Levels based on the Organizations Users accrued spend. The Organization will remain in its starting MVPs Level through that Program Period unless and until its Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases in that same Program Period moves the Organization up into a higher MVPs Level. The highest MVPs Level reached from accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period will be that Organizations starting MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period. If an Organization does not make enough Qualifying Purchases in a given Program Period to maintain its MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period, the Organization will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower MVPs Level corresponding to its accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases in that preceding Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each MVPs Level status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required), Rewards and/or Member Benefits and determine your starting MVPs Level for any Program Period in its sole discretion.</li></ul><ul><ul class="list-circle"><li><b>Summary.</b></li></ul></ul><ul class="list-circle"><ul class="list-circle"><ul><ul class="list-disc"><li>Each Program Period is one year.</li><li>Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period determines which MVPs Level the Organization is in for that Program Period. Users accrued spend resets to zero at the start of each Program Period.</li><li>The MVPs Level the Organization is in at the end of a given Program Period will be the MVPs Level at which the Organization begins the subsequent Program Period, but the Organization can move up into a higher MVPs Level based on Users accrued spend in that subsequent Program Period.</li><li>Organizations do not move down into a lower MVPs Level within the same Program Period. However, an Organization will begin a subsequent Program Period at a lower MVPs Level if the Organizations Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases within the immediately preceding Program Period do not meet the minimum amount required to maintain the same MVPs Level.</li></ul></ul></ul><li><b style="background-color: transparent;">MVPs Earn Back Rewards.</b><span style="background-color: transparent;">&nbsp;</span><b style="background-color: transparent;">MVPs Earn Back Rewards</b><span style="background-color: transparent;"> will be calculated as a percentage of the accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases made during a Program Period by the Organizations Users, and the Organizations accrued reward balance will be available to the Primary Admin in the Organizations Pro Account. MVPs Earn Back Rewards will be issued in the form of electronic Lowes Gift Cards (</span><b style="background-color: transparent;">Lowes E-Gift Card</b><span style="background-color: transparent;"> or </span><b style="background-color: transparent;">E-Gift Card</b><span style="background-color: transparent;">) that will appear in the Primary Admins Wallet once the accrued reward balance is claimed as an E-Gift Card by the Primary Admin on behalf of the Organization. The percentage is determined by the Organizations MVPs Level at the time the Qualifying Purchase was made, except if the amount spent on a specific Qualifying Purchase would result in the Organization moving up to a higher MVPs Level, in which case the percentage will be calculated on a pro rata basis (see example below). Only PRO Tracked Purchases will count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation or MVPs Level determination (i.e., purchases made without using Registered Tender, Member ID or while not signed in to your PRO Account will not count). Paint Qualifying Purchases (as defined below) will not count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation.</span><br></li><ul class="list-circle"><li><b>MVPs Earn Back Rewards Calculation. </b>The MVPs Earn Back Reward amount will be determined in accordance with the graduated percentages in Table 1.1 below. Each MVPs Level and the MVPs Earn Back Reward percentage earned are progressive, meaning the applicable percentage will only apply to the amount spent within the MVPs Level. Lowes will round partial cents to the nearest cent. It is possible for two percentages to be applied to one Qualifying Purchase for the purpose of calculating the Reward. By way of example only, if an Organization needed to accrue $50 in order to move up to a higher MVPs Level and a User spends $100 on a&nbsp;Qualifying Purchase, half of that Qualifying Purchase will be used to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the lower MVPs Level and half will be used to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the higher MVPs Level.</li></ul></ul><ul></ul><br><p></p><p></p><ul class="GridStyles__GridColumn-sc-1ejksnu-2 jVtdnu col sc-1t79ojw_engage-common-1 exSWev sm-12 md-12 lg-12 xl-12"><div class="nvl2lw_engage-common-0 fmiIDq" data-techname="TextBlock" data-businessname="na" data-componenttitle="na" data-triggerimpression="false" data-trigger="false" data-gaugelinkid="&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul class=&quot;list-disc&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font"><h2 class="styles__H2-sc-11vpuyu-1 irzRON typography variant--h2 align--left section-header" color="text_primary"></h2><div data-linkid="&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul class=&quot;list-disc&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font" class="ifxsfn_engage-common-0 eWBThw"><p></p><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Legacy Paint Program Transition.</span> On March 7, 2022, Lowes For Pros Loyalty Paint Rewards Pilot Program members (<span style="font-weight: bold;">Legacy Paint Members</span>) will be transitioned to the MVPs Pro Paint Rewards program. Lowes, in its sole discretion, will determine Legacy Paint Members initial Paint Tier based on the Organizations 2021 spend in the legacy paint program. Lowes, in its sole discretion, will calculate the spend from Jan. 7, 2022, forward to determine the Organizations 2023 starting Paint Tier.</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MVPs Paint Qualifying Purchases. </span>Paint Qualifying Purchases include net completed purchases of only interior paint, exterior paint, exterior stains, floor coatings, primers, resurfacers, barn and fence paint, masonry waterproofers, and marine coatings (collectively <span style="font-weight: bold;">Paint</span>) and subject to the exclusions below (<span style="font-weight: bold;">Paint Qualifying Purchases</span>). Completed purchases means the transaction has been settled and fulfilled and the transaction appears on the Organizations Account purchase history. Paint Qualifying Purchases are PRO Tracked Purchases calculated based on the actual amount paid on any completed purchases of Paint made by the Organization during the Program Period after&nbsp;<span style="background-color: transparent; font-size: unset;">any allowable discounts are applied, if any, excluding shipping and handling; delivery; surcharges; service fees; sales and use taxes; and product fees. Qualifying Purchases do not include (i) mistints; (ii) purchases made using an employee discount; (iii) purchases or transactions made with Rewards or other promotional items (such as free items), whether made in store, online or through the Lowes App; (iv) paint purchases made for personal use, including any purchase using a Personal Account or Military Discount; or (v) paint purchases made on tender previously registered by another Organization.</span></li></ul><ul class="list-circle"><ul class="list-circle"><li>If an item from a Paint Qualifying Purchase is returned, the return amount will be deducted from Paint Qualifying Purchase spend toward earning Paint Rewards. If the item is returned after a Paint Reward has been issued, your Account may reflect a negative balance.</li></ul></ul><p></p><p></p><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="background-color: transparent;"><b>Paint Tiers.</b> Each Organization can reach one or more paint tiers (Paint Tier(s)) based on the accrued spend within a given Program Period from that Organizations Users Paint Qualifying Purchases (as defined below). Details regarding the Paint Tiers are available through the </span><a href="https://www.lowes.com/Pro" style="background-color: transparent;">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page</a><span style="background-color: transparent;">. Upon joining the Program, an Organization will be placed in the lowest Paint Tier. As an Organizations Users make Paint Qualifying Purchases during the applicable Program Period, the Organization may move up into one or more Paint Tier(s) based on the Organizations Users Paint Qualifying Purchase accrued spend. The Organization will remain in its starting Paint Tier through that Program Period unless and until its Users accrued spend on Paint Qualifying Purchases in that same Program Period moves the Organization up into a higher Paint Tier. The highest Paint Tier reached from accrued spend on Paint Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period will be that Organizations starting Paint Tier for the subsequent Program Period. If an Organization does not make enough Paint Qualifying Purchases in a given Program Period to maintain its Paint Tier for the subsequent Program Period, the Organization will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower Paint Tier corresponding to its accrued spend from Paint Qualifying Purchases in that preceding Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each Paint Tier status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required), Rewards and/or Member Benefits and determine your starting Paint Tier for any Program Period in its sole discretion.&nbsp;</span><br></li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Paint Rewards.</span> <b>Paint Rewards</b> will be calculated as a percentage of the spend from Paint Qualifying Purchases made during a Program Period by the Organizations Users, pursuant to the Paint Rewards Calculation described below, and the Organizations accrued reward balance will be available to the Primary Admin in the Organizations Rewards Program dashboard within its Pro Account. Paint Rewards will be issued in the form of electronic Lowes E-Gift Card that will appear in the Primary Admin's Wallet once the accrued reward balance is claimed as an E-Gift Card by the Primary Admin on behalf of the Organization.</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Paint Rewards Calculation. </span>Paint Rewards amount will be determined in accordance with the graduated percentages in Table 1.2 below. Each tier and the reward amount earned are progressive, meaning the applicable percentage will only apply to the amount spent within the Paint Tier. It is possible for two percentages to be applied to one Paint Qualifying Purchase for the purpose of calculating the Paint Reward. Lowes will round partial cents to the nearest cent. By way of example only, if an Organization needed to accrue $50 in order to move up to a higher tier and a User spends $100 on a Paint Qualifying Purchase, half of that Qualifying Purchase will be used to calculate Paint Rewards at the lower tier and half will be used to calculate Paint Rewards at the higher Paint Tier.</li></ul><p></p></div></div></div></div></div></div><div irzRON typography variant--h2 align--left section-header" color="text_primary" id=""></h2><div data-linkid="&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul class=&quot;list-disc&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font" class="ifxsfn_engage-common-0 eWBThw"><p></p><ul class="list-disc"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Claiming of Rewards Issued as Lowes E-Gift Cards.</span> To claim your Organizations Rewards issued as Lowes E-Gift Cards, the Primary Admin must access the available MVPs Pro Rewards dashboard on the Lowes App or online at www.lowes.com to view available accrued reward balance and then claim an available E-Gift Card on behalf of the Organization.&nbsp;An Organization must reach the applicable status or tier before it is eligible to earn or claim Rewards. All available Rewards must be claimed by the end of each Program Period, except that any MVPs Earn Back Rewards or Paint Rewards earned from Qualifying Purchases or Paint Qualifying Purchases (as applicable) made in December may be claimed until January 15 of the following Program Period (or any other time frame as Lowes may determine in its sole discretion) by calling 1-844-LOW4PRO. Rewards do not roll over into any subsequent Program Periods. Any Rewards not claimed by the applicable deadline will be forfeited. Lowes reserves the right, in its sole discretion, to only offer Lowes E-Gift Cards in a minimum amount or in whole-dollar denominations, or as otherwise determined by Lowes. MVPs Earn Back Rewards or Paint Rewards can only be claimed in full, which means the Organization must claim the maximum amount of MVPs Earn Back Rewards or Paint Rewards available to it at the time of claiming. The maximum Lowes E-Gift Card that can be claimed at one time is $2,000. Any accrued reward balance above $2,000 can be claimed with additional E-Gift Card(s). Rewards may be subject to additional terms and will expire in accordance with the terms stated for that Reward. Determinations regarding claiming of Rewards are subject to Lowes sole and absolute discretion. Lowes E-Gift Cards do not expire.&nbsp;</li><ul class="list-circle"><li>The amount of claimed Rewards will be subtracted from the accrued reward balance associated with the Organizations Account immediately when a Reward is requested based on the total Rewards dollars for the claimed Reward. For example, if the Organization has earned $25.30 in Rewards, the Organization must claim $25.30, which will be deducted from the Organizations Account. In the event Lowes determines, in its sole and absolute discretion, that the Reward requested by that Primary Admin is unused and unavailable and the situation justifies restoration, the amount of such requested Reward will be restored to the Organizations Account. Lowes reserves the right to limit the claiming of specific Rewards and to limit the number of Rewards available at any particular MVPs Level.&nbsp;&nbsp;</li></ul><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">MVPs Bonus Points Program.</span>&nbsp;Between July 11, 2022, and December 31, 2024 (unless we extend otherwise), Organizations will have the opportunity to earn and redeem bonus points (<span style="font-weight: bold;">Bonus Points</span>) through the Program. Bonus Points are automatically tracked at the time of the qualifying purchase, transaction or activity as defined by Lowes from time to time (<span style="font-weight: bold;">Points Offers</span> <span style="font-weight: bold;">or</span> <span style="font-weight: bold;">Offerings</span>). Lowes is under no obligation to provide Organizations with any particular number of Points Offers or special offers, or to send messages to such Organizations.&nbsp;</li><ul class="list-disc"><ul class="list-circle"><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Bonus Points.</span>&nbsp;Bonus Points will be credited to the Pro Account upon consummation of the Points Offers. Bonus Points for any Points Offers / Offerings may only be credited to the Organization (1) Pro Account. In certain cases, Bonus Points may not immediately be credited to the Organizations PRO Account. Lowes shall not be responsible for, or liable to, any Organization, User, person or entity, in any way, for any losses, costs or expenses incurred by a delay or error in crediting Bonus Points to an Organizations Pro Account.&nbsp;</li><li>The total Bonus Points available for an Organizations Pro Account will be displayed in the Organizations Pro Account in the App or online at <a href="http://lowes.com/account">lowes.com/account</a>. Organizations cannot combine Bonus Points with or transfer Bonus Points to other Pro Accounts.&nbsp;</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Points Offers or Points Offering: Milestones, Events, Promotional Activities, Etc.</span> From time to time, Lowes, or others acting with our permission, may offer Organizations opportunities to earn Bonus Points for certain Offerings, such as inviting the Organization to engage in certain promotional activities; upon achieving certain Program milestones; redeeming Bonus Points; or other actions or opportunities as may be presented. Bonus Points for such Offerings will be awarded as described in the applicable offer and will be subject to any additional terms set forth within that offer.&nbsp;</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Redeeming Bonus Points for Reward Products or Rewards items.</span>&nbsp;Organizations may have the opportunity to redeem Bonus Points for certain items (<b>Rewards items</b> or <b>Reward Products</b>). To redeem Bonus Points for Rewards items or Reward Products, you must access the Bonus Rewards Center section on the App or online at <a href="https://www.lowes.com/account/mvp/loyalty-benefits?pageId=1" title="https://www.lowes.com/account/mvp/loyalty-benefits?pageId=1" target="_blank">MVPs Pro Rewards Program</a>&nbsp;to view Rewards items or Reward Products available for redemption, and then select to redeem an available Reward. Each Rewards items or Reward Products will indicate the amount of Bonus Points necessary for redemption. You must have enough Bonus Points available in your Lowes PRO Account (<b>Available Points</b>) for the Rewards items or Reward Products you wish to redeem. Bonus Points may only be redeemed for one Rewards Product per transaction and only by the Primary Admin of the Pro Account on behalf of the Organization. You may not redeem your Bonus Points for Rewards items or Reward Products in the same transaction in which the Bonus Points are accrued. Reward Products cannot be redeemed through any third-party platforms. All Rewards items or Reward Products are offers for a limited time, while supplies last, and provided on a first-come, first-served basis. Rewards items or Reward Products can only be redeemed for a limited time as set forth in the Rewards Center. Determinations regarding redemption of Bonus Points are subject to Lowes sole and absolute discretion. Lowes reserves the right to limit the redemption of specific Rewards items or Reward Products and limit the number of Rewards items or Reward Products available for redemption.</li><li>If your transaction for the redemption of Bonus Points for Rewards items or Reward Products within the Rewards Center is not completed in the same visit, the Rewards items or Reward Products will remain in your cart so long as the Reward Product is still available in the Rewards Center.&nbsp;</li><li>Bonus Points will be subtracted from the Organizations Lowes Pro Account immediately when a Rewards items or Reward Products is redeemed. Bonus Points will be restored to a PRO Account only in the event Lowes determines, in its sole and absolute discretion, that the Rewards items or Reward Products requested are unavailable or cannot be delivered.&nbsp;&nbsp;</li><li>Attempts to redeem Bonus Points multiple times or through multiple users constitutes fraud and may result in the termination or suspension of your Lowes Pro Account. If you attempt to use Bonus Points more than once to redeem Rewards items or Reward Products, you may be terminated or suspended from the Bonus Points Program.&nbsp;</li><li>Upon redemption of a Rewards items or Reward Products, Lowes will ship the Rewards items or Reward Products to the address in the Organizations Pro Account or an address provided by the Organization,&nbsp;unless otherwise indicated at the time of redemption. Shipping and handling charges may apply to a redeemed Rewards items or Reward Products. Any attempt to cancel or return a Reward Product or Rewards item will not result in Bonus Points being added back to the Organizations Pro Account. Rewards Products are limited in nature and Lowes cannot guarantee that we will be able to re-ship any Reward Products that you redeemed with your Bonus Points if the Reward Product arrives damaged.&nbsp;&nbsp;</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Return of Purchases Earning Bonus Points.</span> If an Organization returns a purchased item, for which it has garnered Bonus Points, then Lowes reserves the right to deduct such Bonus Points from the Organizations PRO Account. Please note that returning a purchased item may potentially result in a negative balance in your PRO Account. &nbsp;&nbsp;</li><li><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expiration of Bonus Points; Inactive Accounts.</span> An Organization will retain active status in the Program by participating in an Offering or redeeming Bonus Points within a Program Period (Active). (Inactive).&nbsp;</li><li>All unredeemed Bonus Points will expire upon (i) becoming an Inactive participant in the Program, (ii) the cancellation or termination of your Lowes Pro Account as described below, or (iii) the termination of the Bonus Points Program.&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li><li>Whether a participant is Active or Inactive in the Program depends on whether the participant has participated Once a MLR Member reaches a certain MyLowes Rewards Status, the MLR Member will maintain that MyLowes Status for the remainder of the MyLowes Rewards Program Period and the subsequent MyLowes Rewards Program Period provided Eligible Purchases are not returned. If a MLR Member does not make enough Eligible Purchases by the end of a given MyLowes Rewards Program Period to maintain the MyLowes Rewards Status reached the previous MyLowes Reward Program Period, then the MLR Member will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower MyLowes Rewards Status that corresponds to the MLR Members actual accrued spend from Eligible Purchases made in the preceding MyLowes Rewards Program Period. A MLR Members Eligible Purchase accrued spend will reset to zero at the beginning of each new MyLowes Rewards Program Period. Details regarding the MVPs Levels are available through the \u003ca href=\"/l/Pro/pro-benefits\" title=\"/l/Pro/pro-benefits\">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page\u003c/a>. Upon joining the Program, an Organization will be placed in the lowest MVPs Level. As an Organizations Users make Qualifying Purchases during the applicable Program Period, the Organization may move up into one or more MVPs Levels based on the Organizations Users accrued spend. The Organization will remain in its starting MVPs Level through that Program Period unless and until its Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases in that same Program Period moves the Organization up into a higher MVPs Level. The highest MVPs Level reached from accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period will be that Organizations starting MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period. If an Organization does not make enough Qualifying Purchases in a given Program Period to maintain its MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period, the Organization will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower MVPs Level corresponding to its accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases in that preceding Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each MVPs Level status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required), Rewards and/or Member Benefits and determine your starting MVPs Level for any Program Period in its sole discretion.\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003cul>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cli>\u003cb>Summary.\u003c/b>\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cul>\u003cul class=\"list-disc\">\u003cli>Each Program Period is one year.\u003c/li>\u003cli>Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period determines which MVPs Level the Organization is in for that Program Period. Users accrued spend resets to zero at the start of each Program Period.\u003c/li>\u003cli>The MVPs Level the Organization is in at the end of a given Program Period will be the MVPs Level at which the Organization begins the subsequent Program Period, but the Organization can move up into a higher MVPs Level based on Users accrued spend in that subsequent Program Period.\u003c/li>\u003cli>Organizations do not move down into a lower MVPs Level within the same Program Period. However, an Organization will begin a subsequent Program Period at a lower MVPs Level if the Organizations Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases within the immediately preceding Program Period do not meet the minimum amount required to maintain the same MVPs Level.\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003cli>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">MVPs Earn Back Rewards.\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\">&nbsp;\u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">MVPs Earn Back Rewards\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"> will be calculated as a percentage of the accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases made during a Program Period by the Organizations Users, and the Organizations accrued reward balance will be available to the Primary Admin in the Organizations Pro Account. MVPs Earn Back Rewards will be issued in the form of electronic Lowes Gift Cards (\u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">Lowes E-Gift Card\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"> or \u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">E-Gift Card\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\">) that will appear in the Primary Admins Wallet once the accrued reward balance is claimed as an E-Gift Card by the Primary Admin on behalf of the Organization. The percentage is determined by the Organizations MVPs Level at the time the Qualifying Purchase was made, except if the amount spent on a specific Qualifying Purchase would result in the Organization moving up to a higher MVPs Level, in which case the percentage will be calculated on a pro rata basis (see example below). Only PRO Tracked Purchases will count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation or MVPs Level determination (i.e., purchases made without using Registered Tender, Member ID or while not signed in to your PRO Account will not count). Paint Qualifying Purchases (as defined below) will not count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation.\u003c/span>\u003cbr>\u003c/li>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cli>\u003cb>MVPs Earn Back Rewards Calculation. \u003c/b>The MVPs Earn Back Reward amount will be determined in accordance with the graduated percentages in Table 1.1 below. Each MVPs Level and the MVPs Earn Back Reward percentage earned are progressive, meaning the applicable percentage will only apply to the amount spent within the MVPs Level. Lowes will round partial cents to the nearest cent. It is possible for two percentages to be applied to one Qualifying Purchase for the purpose of calculating the Reward. By way of example only, if an Organization needed to accrue $50 in order to move up to a higher MVPs Level and a User spends $100 on a&nbsp;Qualifying Purchase, half of that Qualifying Purchase will be used to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the lower MVPs Level and half will be used to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the higher MVPs Level.\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003cul>\u003c/ul>\u003cbr>\u003cp>\u003c/p>\u003cp>\u003c/p>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003c/ul>\u003cp>\u003c/p>"},"decodedHTML":"\u003ch2>\u003cspan style=\"font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;\">\u003c/span>\u003c/h2>\u003ch2>\u003c/h2>\u003ch2>\u003c/h2>\u003cp>\u003cb style=\"font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;\">PRO Account Specific Benefits.\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"font-size: unset; background-color: transparent;\">A PRO Account may be required to obtain and use certain site features, programs and benefits, including but not limited to the MVPs Pro Rewards & Partnership Program, Bulk Purchasing, and Pro Exclusive Pricing. Details regarding the MVPs Levels are available through the \u003ca href=\"/l/Pro/pro-benefits\" title=\"/l/Pro/pro-benefits\">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page\u003c/a>. Upon joining the Program, an Organization will be placed in the lowest MVPs Level. As an Organizations Users make Qualifying Purchases during the applicable Program Period, the Organization may move up into one or more MVPs Levels based on the Organizations Users accrued spend. The Organization will remain in its starting MVPs Level through that Program Period unless and until its Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases in that same Program Period moves the Organization up into a higher MVPs Level. The highest MVPs Level reached from accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period will be that Organizations starting MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period. If an Organization does not make enough Qualifying Purchases in a given Program Period to maintain its MVPs Level for the subsequent Program Period, the Organization will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower MVPs Level corresponding to its accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases in that preceding Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each MVPs Level status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required), Rewards and/or Member Benefits and determine your starting MVPs Level for any Program Period in its sole discretion.\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003cul>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cli>\u003cb>Summary.\u003c/b>\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cul>\u003cul class=\"list-disc\">\u003cli>Each Program Period is one year.\u003c/li>\u003cli>Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period determines which MVPs Level the Organization is in for that Program Period. Users accrued spend resets to zero at the start of each Program Period.\u003c/li>\u003cli>The MVPs Level the Organization is in at the end of a given Program Period will be the MVPs Level at which the Organization begins the subsequent Program Period, but the Organization can move up into a higher MVPs Level based on Users accrued spend in that subsequent Program Period.\u003c/li>\u003cli>Organizations do not move down into a lower MVPs Level within the same Program Period. However, an Organization will begin a subsequent Program Period at a lower MVPs Level if the Organizations Users accrued spend on Qualifying Purchases within the immediately preceding Program Period do not meet the minimum amount required to maintain the same MVPs Level.\u003c/li>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003c/ul>\u003cli>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">MVPs Earn Back Rewards.\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\">\u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">MVPs Earn Back Rewards\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"> will be calculated as a percentage of the accrued spend from Qualifying Purchases made during a Program Period by the Organizations Users, and the Organizations accrued reward balance will be available to the Primary Admin in the Organizations Pro Account. MVPs Earn Back Rewards will be issued in the form of electronic Lowes Gift Cards (\u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">Lowes E-Gift Card\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"> or \u003c/span>\u003cb style=\"background-color: transparent;\">E-Gift Card\u003c/b>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\">) that will appear in the Primary Admins Wallet once the accrued reward balance is claimed as an E-Gift Card by the Primary Admin on behalf of the Organization. The percentage is determined by the Organizations MVPs Level at the time the Qualifying Purchase was made, except if the amount spent on a specific Qualifying Purchase would result in the Organization moving up to a higher MVPs Level, in which case the percentage will be calculated on a pro rata basis (see example below). Only PRO Tracked Purchases will count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation or MVPs Level determination (i.e., purchases made without using Registered Tender, Member ID or while not signed in to your PRO Account will not count). Paint Qualifying Purchases (as defined below) will not count toward MVPs Earn Back Rewards calculation.\u003c/span>\u003cbr>\u003c/li>\u003cul class=\"list-circle\">\u003cli>\u003cb>MVPs Earn Back Rewards Calculation. \u003c/b>The MVPs Earn Back Reward amount will be determined in accordance with the graduated percentages in Table 1.1 below. Each MVPs Level and the MVPs Earn Back Reward percentage earned are progressive, meaning the applicable percentage will only apply to the amount spent within the MVPs Level. Lowes will round partial cents to the nearest cent. It is possible for two percentages to be applied to one Qualifying Purchase for the purpose of calculating the Reward. to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the lower MVPs Level and half will be used to calculate MVPs Earn Back Rewards at the higher MVPs Details regarding the Paint Tiers are available through the \u003c/span>\u003ca href=\"https://www.lowes.com/Pro\" style=\"background-color: transparent;\">MVPs Pro Rewards Program page\u003c/a>\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\">. Upon joining the Program, an Organization will be placed in the lowest Paint Tier. As an Organizations Users make Paint Qualifying Purchases during the applicable Program Period, the Organization may move up into one or more Paint Tier(s) based on the Organizations Users Paint Qualifying Purchase accrued spend. The Organization will remain in its starting Paint Tier through that Program Period unless and until its Users accrued spend on Paint Qualifying Purchases in that same Program Period moves the Organization up into a higher Paint Tier. The highest Paint Tier reached from accrued spend on Paint Qualifying Purchases during a given Program Period will be that Organizations starting Paint Tier for the subsequent Program Period. If an Organization does not make enough Paint Qualifying Purchases in a given Program Period to maintain its Paint Tier for the subsequent Program Period, the Organization will begin the subsequent Program Period at the lower Paint Tier corresponding to its accrued spend from Paint Qualifying Purchases in that preceding Program Period. Lowes reserves the right to change, modify or update the requirements needed to earn each Paint Tier status (including, without limitation, the minimum amount of accrued spend required), Rewards and/or Member Benefits and determine your starting Paint Tier for any Program Period in its sole discretion.&nbsp;\u003c/span>\u003cbr>\u003c/li>\u003cli>\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: bold;\">Paint Rewards.\u003c/span> \u003cb>Paint Rewards\u003c/b> will be calculated as a percentage of the spend from Paint Qualifying Purchases made during a Program Period by the Organizations Users, pursuant to the Paint Rewards Calculation described below, and the Organizations accrued reward balance will be available to the Primary Admin in the Organizations Rewards Program dashboard within its Pro Account.
